\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00082}00082 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef TRANSLATOR\_FR\_H}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00083}00083 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define TRANSLATOR\_FR\_H}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00084}00084 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00085}00085 \textcolor{comment}{// When defining a translator class for the new language, follow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00086}00086 \textcolor{comment}{// the description in the documentation.  One of the steps says}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00087}00087 \textcolor{comment}{// that you should copy the translator\_en.h (this) file to your}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00088}00088 \textcolor{comment}{// translator\_xx.h new file.  Your new language should use the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00089}00089 \textcolor{comment}{// Translator class as the base class.  This means that you need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00090}00090 \textcolor{comment}{// implement exactly the same (pure virtual) methods as the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00091}00091 \textcolor{comment}{// TranslatorEnglish does.  Because of this, it is a good idea to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00092}00092 \textcolor{comment}{// start with the copy of TranslatorEnglish and replace the strings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00093}00093 \textcolor{comment}{// one by one.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00094}00094 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00095}00095 \textcolor{comment}{// It is not necessary to include "{}translator.h"{} or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00096}00096 \textcolor{comment}{// "{}translator\_adapter.h"{} here.  The files are included in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00097}00097 \textcolor{comment}{// language.cpp correctly.  Not including any of the mentioned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00098}00098 \textcolor{comment}{// files frees the maintainer from thinking about whether the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00099}00099 \textcolor{comment}{// first, the second, or both files should be included or not, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00100}00100 \textcolor{comment}{// why.  This holds namely for localized translators because their}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00101}00101 \textcolor{comment}{// base class is changed occasionally to adapter classes when the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{// Translator class changes the interface, or back to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00103}00103 \textcolor{comment}{// Translator class (by the local maintainer) when the localized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{// translator is made up-\/to-\/date again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00105}00105 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__fr_8h_source_l00106}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_translator_french}{00106}} \textcolor{keyword}{class }\mbox{\hyperlink{class_translator_french}{TranslatorFrench}} : \textcolor{keyword}{public} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_translator_adapter__1__9__5}{TranslatorAdapter\_1\_9\_5}}}
